upplementary Credit Data Sheet
Section I - Timetable of Key Processing Events
(a) Time taken by country to prepare credit: About 18 months
(b) Credit prepared by:                       Government with assistance
from UNESCOICP,
consultants & IDA
(c) First IDA mission:                        March 1987 (ident.)
(d) Departure of appraisal mission:           July 1988
Ce) Negotiations completeds                   End April 1989
(f) Planned date of effectiveness:            August 1989
Cg) List of relevant PCRs and PPARss          - First Education Project
(Cr.420-MLI)
PCR: Jan.11, 1982
Second Education Project
(Cr.733-MLI)
PCR: June 1985
PPAR: Oct. 8, 1986
Section II - Key Documents orovided at nesotiations
Ci) 1989 budget; (ii) draft legal text revising the budget nomenclature;
Ciii) draft legal text reorganizing the PCU.
Section III - Points covered at negotiations
Mi) Status of rationalization of IPEGs and ENSECs (para. 48);
(ii) criteria for higher education scholarships award and renewal
(para. 51); (iii) 1989 budget and proposed nomenclature revision
(para. 51); (iv) preparation of the 1990 Staffing Plan (para. 52);
(v) investment program (para. 55); (vi) experience with NGO-
cofinanced prototype construction and FAEF operating rules (para.
54); (vii) Government proposed textbook policy (para. 73); (viii) new
organization of the PCU (para. 83); (ix) implementation and
monitoring arrangements (para. 93); (x) TORs for the twinning
institutions (para. 95); (xi) first year program of activities and
budget (para. 105); (xii) arrangements for the quick disbursements
from various cofinancing sources; and (xiii) schedule of negotiations
with other cofinanciers.



- 118 -                    ANNEX XII
Page 2 of 4
Section IV - Special IDA Implementation Actions
(a) Disbursement of US$1.5 million in a Special Account as credit
effectiveness and related disbursement conditions are fulfilled
(para. 104);
(b) Joint Annual Review of Program and Project implementation, to be held
no later than November 30. each year starting in 1989 through the
life of the Project. (para. 105);
Section V - Conditions of Board Presentation
(a) Signature of the Letter of Education Policy by the Minister of Labor
on behalf of the Minister of Education (para. 44);
Section VI - Conditions of Effectiveness. Disbursement and Tranche
Release
(a) Conditions of Effectiveness and First Tranche Releaset
Mi)      Modification of MEN's budget nomenclature to separate Cycle
I from Cycle II budgets, and reclassify as such the
,materials* element of secondary education scholarships
(para. 51);
(ii)      Legal establishment of the FAEF (para. 54);
(iii)     Reorganization of the PCU (para. 83);
(iv)      Fulfillment of the conditions precedent to effectiveness of
the cofinancing by USAID (para. 86); and
(v)       Signature of the contract for the Technical Advisor to the
Project Director (para. 86);
(b) Conditions of disbursement:
(i)       For the primary school construction/rehabilitation
components signature of the contract with a Volunteers
Association (para. 63);
(ii)      For the experimental Line of Creditz reinforcement of
UNDP/ILO Unit to IDA's satisfaction (para. 77);
(iii)     For the sector management component: signature of the
twinning contract with an Institute for Educational
Economics Research, acceptable to IDA (para. 79 and 80);
(c) Conditions of Second Tranche Release:
(i)       Measure 14:  (a) agreement on a utilization plan for ENSEC
facilities; (b) issuance of decree modifying the
recruitment level and duration of studies at IPEG; (c)



- 119 -                    AMflE XII
Page 3 of 4
introduction of agreed-upon revised IPEG curriculum by the
beginning of school year 1990191 (para. 48);
(ii)      Measure #6:  Agreement on a detailed Master Plan for
restructuring secondary and higher education in line with
the parameters defined in the Letter of Education Policy
(para. 50);
(iii)     Measure 17:  Satisfactory progress toward the budgetary
targets: budget laws for 1989 (ex-post) and 1990 (ex-ante)
(a) maintaining the share of MEN in the Government
recurrent budget at least at 252; (b) increasing the share
of primary education to about 40? of MEN's recurrent
budget; (c) increasing the share of materials to about 8?
of MEN's budget; (d) reducing higher education scholarships
(Mali and abroad) by 10? in 1989 and 1O? in 1990 (current
terms); and (e) maintaining the share of higher education
below 192 of MEN's recurrent budget (para. 51);
(iv)      Measure #8S:  (a) Studentsiteacher ratio increased from 38:1
to at least 39s1 in Cycle I, from 14:1 to at least 18:1 for
Cycle II and from 8:1 to at least 10:1 for secondary
education; (b) personnel study reviewed with IDA, including
proposals to reduce the number of Cycle II and secondary
teachers and appropriate levels of civil service
recruitment for IPEG and ENSEC graduates (para. 53);
Cd) Conditions for Third Tranche Releaset
i)        Measure #5: Agreement with IDA on a work program for the
Task Force on curriculum adaptation, taking into account
the findings of an evaluation of ruralization and national
languages experiments discussed with IDA (para. 49);
(ii)      Measure #6:  Satisfactory progress in implementing the
agreed-upon Master Plan for restructuring secondary and
higher education (para. 50);
(iii)     Measure #7:  Continued satisfactory progress toward the
budgetary targets; budget laws for 1990 (ex-post) and 1991
(ex-ante) (a) maintaining the share of MEN in the
Government recurrent budget at least at 25?; (b) increasing
the share of primary education to at least 42? of MEN's
budget; (c) increasing the share of materials to at least
9? of MEN's budget; (d) reducing higher education
scholarships by 10? in 1990, and 5? in 1991; and (e)
maintaining the share of higher education below 19? of
MEN's recurrent budget (para. 51);
(iv)      Measure #8t  (a) Students/teacher ratio increased to at
least 40:1 in Cycle I, 20:1 in Cycle II and 12:1 in
secondary education; (b) implementation of agreed-upon



ANNEX XII
Page 4 of 4
recommendations of the personnel study along an agreed-upon
schedule (para. 53);
Section VII- Assurances to be received from Government:
(a) Measure #1: During school years 1989190 through 1991/92, the number
of new entrants would be maintained, for secondary general education,
below an average of 2,500, and for higher education, below a total of
4,500 over the three-year period, or an average of 1,500 p.a.
(students in Mali and abroad) (para. 45);
(b) By the 1989 Joint Annual Review, Government would issue norms and
regulations for the private educational sector (para. 46);
(c) By March 31, 1990, Government would submit to IDA for discussion, a
study on gender issues making recommendations for improving female
enrollments and women's participation in the teaching corps (para.
47);
(d) Any new sectoral investment in excess of CFAF 300 million would be
reviewed and agreed upon with IDA on the basis of an economic and
financial study (para. 51)
(e) Government would ensure that, starting on January 1, 1990, at least
302 of the revenues from the Development Tax would be earmarked for
the financing of educational activities (para. 54);
(f) Government would, starting in 1989, (i) by November 30 each year,
exchange views with IDA on Implementation of the Project, including
the sectoral adjustment Program; (ii) by September 30 each year, send
in a form and substance satisfactory to IDA a progress report on the
Project and the Program, its revised three-year rolling Program of
Investments and Public expenditures and its draft budget for the
following fiscal year (para. 105);
(g)  (i) All project accounts, including disbursements against SOEs, would
be audited annually by an independent auditor acceptable to IDA; (ii)
Government would submit such reports to IDA by March 31 of each year,
starting in 1990; (iii) the audit reports would certify that the
funds were used for the purposes for which they were provided; (iv)
the PCU would submits (a) semi-annual reports on project
implementation and expenditures by June 30 and December 31 of each
year, beginning in 1989; (b) a completion report within six months of
the IDA Credit closing date (para. 106).
The conditions for second and third Tranche release are expected to be met
respectively by end-November 1990 and 1991.
